        <strong><u>Company Description<br><br></u></strong>Vendavo powers the shift to digital business for the worldâ€™s most demanding B2B companies, unlocking value, growing margin and accelerating revenue with our SaaS products. With an annual margin improvement totaling more than $2.5 billion across companies in chemicals, distribution, high-tech, and manufacturing. Vendavo is headquartered in Denver, CO and has offices around the globe.<br><br>Sell more. Profitably.<br><br><strong><u>Job Description<br><br></u></strong>As a Software Engineer you will be responsible for enhancing the <strong>CPQ platform</strong> by delivering new features and functionality. Development activities will require the candidate to work with <strong>React, RESTful API endpoints, Azure DevOps, SQL Server, and IIS</strong>. This position will also be responsible for extending the platformâ€™s automated testing capabilities and bug fixes to the core platform based on internal testing.<br><ul><li>Design and implementation of new product features</li><li>Provide core support for Vendavoâ€™s CPQ platform</li><li>Enhance the existing CPQ library of Automated Unit and UI Tests</li><li>Knowledge and experience with React</li><li>Knowledge and experience with .NET, C#, MVC, and JavaScript is recommended<br></li></ul><strong><u>Qualifications<br></u></strong><ul><li>Object-oriented development experience</li><li>React web development experience</li><li>Experience developing Unit Tests</li><li>Experience with iterative development methodologies</li><li>Familiar with XML</li><li>Highly developed organizational skills</li><li>Highly developed, process-oriented skills for troubleshooting, problem solving, and problem resolution<br></li></ul>Additional Information<br><br><strong><u>We Are Offering<br></u></strong><ul><li>Working within a team of friendly skilled people where help is always in reach</li><li>Professional growth and development opportunities</li><li>Use of modern tools and access to experts</li><li>Team spirit in the workplace, with weekend retreats and fun team activities</li><li>Opportunities to learn a new field and get a deep understanding of enterprise tech</li><li>Flexible working hours without micromanagement</li><li>Personal freedom and focus on individual responsibility</li><li>Company sponsored events for employees, volunteer tech talks and tournaments</li><li>Weekly English classes, international travel opportunities</li><li>25 days of paid vacation + 2 days paid for charity activities</li><li>Monthly benefits allowance, meal contributions</li><li>MultiSport card available</li><li>Modern cozy offices in Prague, Hradec Kralove and Ostrava, no large open-space floors or cubicles, rec room with games and books</li><li>High-end laptop and smartphone, including personal use</li><li>Option to use discounted unlimited mobile plan for family members</li></ul>
